  262. 138. Mathbox for Kunhao Zheng
    1. 138.1. Weighted AM-GM inequality

MetaMath theorems

Sum of nonnegative extended reals

Constants


sum^

Extend class notation to include the sum of nonnegative extended reals.

Axiom: csumge0


class sum^

Disjoint


w x y

Define the arbitrary sum of nonnegative extended reals. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 17-Aug-2020.) $.

Axiom: df-sumge0


|- sum^ = ( x e. _V |-> if ( +oo e. ran x , +oo , sup ( ran ( y e. ( ~P dom x i^i Fin ) |-> sum_ w e. y ( x ` w ) ) , RR* , < ) ) )

Disjoint


X x y

Disjoint


ph x y

Essential: sge0rnre.1


|- ( ph -> F : X --> ( 0 [,) +oo ) )

When sum^ is applied to nonnegative real numbers the range used in its definition is a subset of the reals. (Contributed by Glauco Siliprandi, 17-Aug-2020.)

Theorem: sge0rnre


|- ( ph -> ran ( x e. ( ~P X i^i Fin ) |-> sum_ y e. x ( F ` y ) ) C_ RR )
